				<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading pagetitle page-header">
					Meine Seufzer, meine Tränen, BWV 13 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)				</h1>	

				<div class="body"><div lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div class="wp_header">
<table>
<table>

<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>6 movements
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composition Year
</th>
<td>1726 in Leipzig
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Genre Categories<span class="addpagetag mh555"></span>
</th>

<td>BWV 13&#160;; BC A 34

</th>
<td>IJB 399
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Key
</th>
<td>D minor
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>6 movements:
<ol><li>Aria (tenor): Meine Seufzer, meine Tränen (D&#160;minor)
</li><li>Recitative (alto): Mein liebster Gott lässt mich annoch (B<span class="music-symbol" style="font-family: Arial Unicode MS, Lucida Sans Unicode; font-size:110%">&#x266d;</span>&#160;major)
</li><li>Chorale (alto): Der Gott, der mir hat versprochen (F&#160;major)
</li><li>Recitative (soprano): Mein Kummer nimmet zu (F&#160;major)
</li><li>Aria (bass): Ächzen und erbärmlich Weinen (G&#160;minor)
</li><li>Chorale: So sei nun, Seele, deine (B<span class="music-symbol" style="font-family: Arial Unicode MS, Lucida Sans Unicode; font-size:110%">&#x266d;</span>&#160;major)
</li></ol>
</td></tr>
<tr>

</td></tr>
